####Fate of France
event = {
	id = 1000510
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = {
		event = 2003047 # German 1940 diplomatic offensive
		event = 2003002 # Armistice at Rethondes
		NOT = { event = 2003049 } # France has not accepted early entry into the Axis during Meeting at Montoire
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = FRA } } 
		NOT = { alliance = { country = GER country = FRA } } #Disable if France and GER are allied
		NOT = { alliance = { country = GER country = U55 } } #Disable if French State and GER are allied
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = JAP } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = SOV country = JAP } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = ENG country = JAP } }
	}
	
	decision_trigger = {
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 55 size = 1 } #At least 1 unit stationed in Paris
		OR = {
			NOT = { war = { country = GER country = ENG } }
			AND = {
					region = { region = England country = -3 data = 1 } #Control all of England
					region = { region = Scotland country = -3 data = 1 } #Control all of Scotland
			}
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		event = 2003047 # German 1940 diplomatic offensive
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = ENG } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = JAP } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = FRA } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = SOV country = JAP } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = ENG country = JAP } }
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 }
	}

	name = 1000510name
	desc = 1000510desc
	style = 2
  	picture = "fateoffrancecolor"
	decision_picture = "fateoffrancedecision"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 3
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = "1000510a"
		ai_chance = 0
		#Gain German national provinces (just in case - should be redundant)
		command = { type = addcore which = 104 } #Metz
		command = { type = addcore which = 105 } #Colmar
		command = { type = addcore which = 107 } #Strasbourg
		command = { type = addcore which = 109 } #Luxembourg
		command = { type = addcore which = 110 } #Eupen
		#Remove German claims on France 
		command = { type = secederegion which = GER value = France when = 2 } #Ensures that Germany owns ALL of France region before commands fire

		command = { type = removeclaim which = 38 } #Rennes
		command = { type = removeclaim which = 39 } #Lorient

#### Fate of Benelux
event = {
    id = 1000511
    random = no
    country = GER
	
	#Triggered by 1000510
	
    name = 1000511name
    desc = 1000511desc
    style = 2
    picture = "fateofbenelux"

    action = {
		name = 1000511a #Create RK states
		ai_chance = 80
		command = { type = dissent value = -1 }
		#Border cleanup just in case player released states already - inherit non-RK puppet states
		command = { trigger = { ispuppet = FLA } type = inherit which = FLA value = 1 } #Inherit Flanders
		command = { trigger = { ispuppet = WLL } type = inherit which = WLL value = 1 } #Inherit Wallonia
		command = { trigger = { ispuppet = HOL } type = inherit which = HOL value = 1 } #Inherit Netherlands
		command = { trigger = { ispuppet = BEL } type = inherit which = BEL value = 1 } #Inherit Belgium
		#Ensure that the two RKs are created if they do not already exist 
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { exists = U46 } } type = independence which = U46 value = 1 } #RK Niederlande
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { exists = U47 } } type = independence which = U47 value = 1 } #RK Belgien-Nordfrankreich	
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { ispuppet = U46 } } type = make_puppet which = U46 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { ispuppet = U47 } } type = make_puppet which = U47 }
		#Cede appropriate provinces to the two RKs
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U46 value = 121 when = 2 }	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U46 value = 123 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U46 value = 118 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U46 value = 120 when = 2 }	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U46 value = 125 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U46 value = 122 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U46 value = 119 when = 2 }	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U46 value = 124 when = 2 }	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U47 value = 117 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U47 value = 115 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U47 value = 116 when = 2 }	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U47 value = 114 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U47 value = 108 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U47 value = 111 when = 2 }	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U47 value = 112 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U47 value = 113 when = 2 }
		#Give RK Belgien-Nordfrankreich (if it exists) northern France
		command = { trigger = { exists = U47 } type = secedeprovince which = U47 value = 49 when = 2 }	
		command = { trigger = { exists = U47 } type = secedeprovince which = U47 value = 51 when = 2 }
		command = { trigger = { exists = U47 } type = secedeprovince which = U47 value = 52 when = 2 }
		command = { type = event which = 1000512 where = GER when = 2 }
    }
	
	action = {
		name = 1000511b
		ai_chance = 20
		#This option allows the player to create Flanders, Wallonia, and the Netherlands if they don't want to create RK states
		command = { type = dissent value = -1 }
		#Border cleanup just in case player released states already
		command = { trigger = { ispuppet = U46 } type = inherit which = U46 value = 1 } #Inherit RK Belgien
		command = { trigger = { ispuppet = U47 } type = inherit which = U47 value = 1 } #Inherit RK Niederlande
		command = { trigger = { ispuppet = BEL } type = inherit which = BEL value = 1 } #Inherit Belgium
		#Create Flanders, Wallonia and Netherlands	
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { exists = FLA } } type = independence which = FLA value = 1 } #Flanders
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { exists = WLL } } type = independence which = WLL value = 1 } #Wallonia
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { ispuppet = FLA } } type = make_puppet which = FLA }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { ispuppet = WLL } } type = make_puppet which = WLL }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { exists = HOL } } type = independence which = HOL value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { ispuppet = HOL } } type = make_puppet which = HOL }
		#Cede appropriate provinces to Flanders, Wallonia and RK Niederlande
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = HOL value = 121 when = 2 }	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = HOL value = 123 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = HOL value = 118 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = HOL value = 120 when = 2 }	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = HOL value = 125 when = 2 }

		command = { type = secedeprovince which = HOL value = 119 when = 2 }	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = HOL value = 124 when = 2 }	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = FLA value = 117 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = FLA value = 115 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = FLA value = 116 when = 2 }	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = FLA value = 114 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = WLL value = 108 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = WLL value = 111 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = WLL value = 112 when = 2 }		
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = WLL value = 113 when = 2 }
		#Ensure Flanders and Wallonia receive northern France before French State is released
		command = { type = addclaim which = 49 where = FLA }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 51 where = FLA }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 52 where = WLL }
		command = { trigger = { exists = FLA } type = secedeprovince which = FLA value = 49 when = 2 }
		command = { trigger = { exists = FLA } type = secedeprovince which = FLA value = 51 when = 2 }

    }
	
    action = {

		command = { trigger = { ispuppet = BEL } type = inherit which = BEL value = 0 } #Belgium
		command = { trigger = { exists = FLA } type = inherit which = FLA value = 0 } #Flanders
		command = { trigger = { exists = WLL } type = inherit which = WLL value = 0 } #Wallonia		
		command = { trigger = { exists = U46 } type = inherit which = U46 value = 0 } #RK Niederlande
		command = { trigger = { exists = U47 } type = inherit which = U47 value = 0 } #RK Belgien-Nordfrankreich	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 49 when = 2 }	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 51 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 52 when = 2 }
		#Add claims on Benelux
		command = { type = addclaim which = 111 }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 112 }

#### Creation of SS-Ordensstaat Burgund
event = {
    id = 1000513
    random = no
    country = GER
	
	#Triggered by 1000512
	
    name = 1000513name
    desc = 1000513desc
    style = 2
    picture = "ssburgundy"

    action = {
		name = 1000513a
		trigger = { alliance = { country = GER country = ITA } }
		#Create SS-Ordensstaat Burgund, revoke Italian gains
		command = { type = relation which = U01 value = -75 }
		command = { type = belligerence which = GER value = 20 }
		command = { type = relation which = ITA value = -50 }
		command = { type = independence which = U52 value = 1 } #SS-Ordenstaat Burgund (new TAG)
		command = { type = make_puppet which = U52 } 
		command = { trigger = { alliance = { country = GER country = ITA } } type = secedeprovince which = U52 value = 87 when = 2 } #Nice
		command = { trigger = { alliance = { country = GER country = ITA } } type = secedeprovince which = U52 value = 91 when = 2 } #Chambery
		command = { type = event which = 1000514 where = GER when = 2 } 
    }
	
	action = {
		name = 1000513b
		trigger = { alliance = { country = GER country = ITA } }
		#Create SS-Ordensstaat Burgund, allow Italy to keep gains
		command = { type = relation which = U01 value = -75 }
		command = { type = belligerence which = GER value = 20 }
		command = { type = relation which = ITA value = 10 }
		command = { type = independence which = U52 value = 1 } #SS-Ordenstaat Burgund (new TAG)
		command = { type = make_puppet which = U52 } 
		command = { type = event which = 1000514 where = GER when = 2 } 
    }
	
	action = {
		name = 1000513c
		trigger = { NOT = { alliance = { country = GER country = ITA } } }
		#Create SS-Ordensstaat Burgund, option exists just in case GER is not allied with ITA
		command = { type = relation which = U01 value = -75 }		
		command = { type = belligerence which = GER value = 20 }
		command = { type = independence which = U52 value = 1 } #SS-Ordenstaat Burgund (new TAG)
		command = { type = make_puppet which = U52 } 
		command = { type = event which = 1000514 where = GER when = 2 } 
    }
	
	action = {
		name = 1000513d
		#Create SS-Ordensstaat Burgund but with much more limited borders
		command = { type = relation which = U01 value = -30 }	
		command = { type = belligerence which = GER value = 5 }
		command = { type = independence which = U52 value = 1 } #SS-Ordenstaat Burgund (new TAG)
		command = { type = make_puppet which = U52 } 
		#Return provinces to GER so that the French State receives them during final partition event
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { control = { province = 87 data = ITA } } } type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 87 when = 2 } #Return Nice if Italy does NOT own it
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { control = { province = 91 data = ITA } } } type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 91 when = 2 } #Return Chambery if Italy does NOT own it
		command = { trigger = { control = { province = 49 data = GER } } type = secedeprovince which = U52 value = 49 when = 2 } #Give Calais if Germany owns it (means RK Belgium does not exist)
		command = { trigger = { control = { province = 51 data = GER } } type = secedeprovince which = U52 value = 51 when = 2 } #Give Dunkirk if Germany owns it (means RK Belgium does not exist)
		command = { trigger = { control = { province = 52 data = GER } } type = secedeprovince which = U52 value = 52 when = 2 } #Give Lille if Germany owns it (means RK Belgium does not exist)
		#Extra land claimed by SS Burgundy
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 90 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 93 when = 2 }		
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 86 when = 2 }		
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 89 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 82 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 78 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 92 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 85 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 88 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 64 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 63 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 63 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 54 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 56 when = 2 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 53 when = 2 }
		command = { type = event which = 1000514 where = GER when = 2 } 
    }
	
    action = {
		name = 1000513e
		#Don't create Ordenstaat, move to next phase of partition

#### The French State
event = {
    id = 1000514
    random = no
    country = GER
	
	#Triggered by 1000513
	
    name = 1000514name
    desc = 1000514desc
    style = 2
    picture = "stateoffrance"

    action = {
		name = 1000514a
		command = { type = dissent value = -1 }
		command = { type = relation which = U01 value = -30 }
		#Create the French State
		command = { type = independence which = U55 value = 1 } #French State (new TAG)
		command = { type = make_puppet which = U55 } 
		#In case GER decided to annex the Benelux RK states, retain Northern France to prevent odd borders
		command = { trigger = { control = { province = 55 data = U55 } NOT = { exists = U47 } NOT = { exists = FLA } NOT = { exists = WLL } } type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 49 when = 2 }
		command = { trigger = { control = { province = 55 data = U55 } NOT = { exists = U47 } NOT = { exists = FLA } NOT = { exists = WLL } } type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 51 when = 2 }
		command = { trigger = { control = { province = 55 data = U55 } NOT = { exists = U47 } NOT = { exists = FLA } NOT = { exists = WLL } } type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 52 when = 2 }
		#War reparations
		command = { type = trade which = GER where = U55 supplies = 10 when = 730 value = 1 }
		command = { type = trade which = GER where = U55 money = 2 when = 730 value = 1 }
		#Reward to the player
		command = { type = morale which = land value = 1 }
		command = { type = morale which = air value = 1 }
		command = { type = morale which = naval value = 1 }
		#Trigger inheritance of FRA tag event for U55
		command = { type = trigger which = 1000730 } 
    }
	
	action = {
		name = 1000514b
		#Leave France occupied 
		command = { type = dissent value = 30 }
		command = { type = belligerence which = GER value = 50 }
    }
}

#### Generalplan Ost - First Phase
event = {
	id = 1000602
	random = no
	country = GER
	save_date = yes

	decision = {
		event = 1000601 #Victory parade in Berlin 
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		ispuppet = U40
		ispuppet = U41
		ispuppet = U42
		ispuppet = U43
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		control = { province = 232 data = U44 } # Warsaw
		control = { province = 264 data = U40 } # Riga
		control = { province = 553 data = U43 } # Leningrad
		control = { province = 572 data = U43 } # Moscow
		control = { province = 617 data = U41 } # Kiev
		control = { province = 663 data = U41 } # Stalingrad
		control = { province = 706 data = U42 } # Astrakhan
	}
	
	decision_trigger = {
		manpower = 1500
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 232 size = 3 } #At least 3 units stationed in Warsaw
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 264 size = 3 } #At least 3 units stationed in Riga
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 553 size = 3 } #At least 3 units stationed in Leningrad
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 572 size = 3 } #At least 3 units stationed in Moscow
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 617 size = 3 } #At least 3 units stationed in Kiev
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 663 size = 3 } #At least 3 units stationed in Stalingrad
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 709 size = 3 } #At least 3 units stationed in Tblisi
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = "Baltic States" country = -3 data = 1 } #All territories ceded from the Bitter Peace must be controlled, forces player to defeat all rebels
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Belarus country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = "Western Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Russia country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = "Southern Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Ukraine country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Kaukasus country = -3 data = 1 }
		area = { area = Arkhangelsk country = -3 data = 1 }
		owned = { province = 548 data = -3 } #Vologda
	}
	
	trigger = { 
		event = 1000601 #Victory parade in Berlin
		OR = {
			NOT = { exists = SOV }
			land_percentage = { country = SOV value = 2.75 }
			}
		NOT = { exists = ENG }
		OR = {
		NOT = { exists = USA }
		AND = {
			land_percentage = { country = USA value = 2.0 }
			naval_percentage = { country = USA value = 0.5 }
			}
		}
		ispuppet = U40
		ispuppet = U41
		ispuppet = U42
		ispuppet = U43
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		control = { province = 232 data = U44 } # Warsaw
		control = { province = 264 data = U40 } # Riga
		control = { province = 553 data = U43 } # Leningrad
		control = { province = 572 data = U43 } # Moscow
		control = { province = 617 data = U41 } # Kiev
		control = { province = 663 data = U41 } # Stalingrad
		control = { province = 706 data = U42 } # Astrakhan 
		region = { region = England country = -3 data = 1 } #Control all of England
		region = { region = Scotland country = -3 data = 1 } #Control all of Scotland
		}

	name = 1000602name
	desc = 1000602desc
	style = 2
	picture = "generalplanost"
	decision_picture = "generalplanostdecision"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1940 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		name = 1000602a
		ai_chance = 99
		command = { type = wartime_ic_mod value = -50 }
		command = { type = peacetime_ic_mod value = -25 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = manpowerpool value = -1500 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = free_manpower value = -0.2 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = money value = -1000 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = manpowerpool value = 500 } #Reward AI with a manpower cheat if it won against SOV; ensures we get a longer game vs US instead of idling
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = free_manpower value = 0.2 }
		command = { type = free_money value = -0.5 }
		command = { type = free_supplies value = -50 }
		command = { type = free_energy value = -100 }
		command = { type = free_metal value = -50 }
		command = { type = free_rare_materials value = -20 }
		command = { type = free_oil value = -100 }
		command = { type = energypool value = -100000 }
		command = { type = metalpool value = -50000 }
		command = { type = rarematerialspool value = -5000 }
		command = { type = oilpool value = -10000 }
		command = { type = setflag which = GeneralPlanOst } #Flag set for future Generalplan Ost decisions and events
	}
	
	action = {
		name = 1000602b
		ai_chance = 1
		command = { } #Do not set GeneralPlanOst flag
	}
}

#### Generalplan Ost - Pacification of the East
event = {
	id = 1000603
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = {
		flag = GeneralPlanOst #Generalplan Ost activated
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		ispuppet = U40
		ispuppet = U41
		ispuppet = U42
		ispuppet = U43
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		control = { province = 232 data = -3 } # Warsaw
		control = { province = 264 data = -3 } # Riga
		control = { province = 553 data = -3 } # Leningrad
		control = { province = 572 data = -3 } # Moscow
		control = { province = 617 data = -3 } # Kiev
		control = { province = 663 data = -3 } # Stalingrad
		control = { province = 709 data = -3 } # Tblisi
	}
	
	decision_trigger = {
		event = { id = 1000602 days = 30 } #One month after Generalplan Ost to give player time to get forces in position
		#German player will be encouraged to keep friendly divisions in all conquered territory to handle rebellions, this acts as a setup event to help player move forces to general regions before revolt takes place.
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 264 type = land size = 6 area = 2 }  # Riga, Baltic States region
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 232 type = land size = 6 area = 2 }  # Warsaw, Poland region
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 599 type = land size = 6 area = 2 }  # Minsk, Belarus region
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 589 type = land size = 6 area = 2 }  # Smolensk, Western Russia region
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 572 type = land size = 6 area = 2 }  # Moscow, Central Russia region
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 604 type = land size = 6 area = 2 }  # Kursk, Southern Russian region
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 617 type = land size = 6 area = 2 }  # Kiev, Ukraine region
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 713 type = land size = 6 area = 2 }  # Baku, Caucasus region
	}
	
	trigger = { 
		flag = GeneralPlanOst #Generalplan Ost activated
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		ispuppet = U40
		ispuppet = U41
		ispuppet = U42
		ispuppet = U43
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		control = { province = 232 data = -3 } # Warsaw
		control = { province = 264 data = -3 } # Riga
		control = { province = 553 data = -3 } # Leningrad
		control = { province = 572 data = -3 } # Moscow
		control = { province = 617 data = -3 } # Kiev
		control = { province = 663 data = -3 } # Stalingrad
		control = { province = 709 data = -3 } # Tblisi
	} #Disable AI from taking this decision

	name = 1000603name
	desc = 1000603desc
	style = 2
	picture = "pacifyeast"
	decision_picture = "pacifyeastdecision"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 20
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		name = 1000603a
        command = { type = dissent value = 5 }		
		command = { type = event which = 1000605 where = GER when = 30 } #Flavor event for German player to inform them of mass uprising in the east
		command = { type = event which = 1000604 where = U40 when = 30 } #Trigger event Existential conflict for all RK states one month from taking decision
		command = { type = event which = 1000604 where = U41 when = 30 } #Trigger event Existential conflict for all RK states one month from taking decision
		command = { type = event which = 1000604 where = U42 when = 30 } #Trigger event Existential conflict for all RK states one month from taking decision
		command = { type = event which = 1000604 where = U43 when = 30 } #Trigger event Existential conflict for all RK states one month from taking decision
	}
}

#### Existential conflict
event = {
    id = 1000604
    random = no
    tag = { U40 U41 U42 U43 } #RK states
	persistent = yes
	
	#Triggered by 1000603

    name = 1000604name
    desc = 1000604desc
    style = 2
    picture = "pacifyeast"

    action = {
		name = 1000604a
		command = { type = dissent value = 70 }	#Ensures province revolt risk will stay high for a long time
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 when = 0 }	
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 when = 0 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 when = 0 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 when = 0 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 when = 0 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 when = 0 }

#### Calm after the Storm
event = {
    id = 1000606
    random = no
    country = GER
	save_date = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		#ai = no 
		event = 1000605 #Event Uprising in the East has happened
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = "Baltic States" country = -3 data = 1 } #All territories ceded from the Bitter Peace must be controlled, forces player to defeat all rebels
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Belarus country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = "Western Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Russia country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = "Southern Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Ukraine country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Kaukasus country = -3 data = 1 }
		area = { area = Arkhangelsk country = -3 data = 1 }
		owned = { province = 548 data = -3 } #Vologda
	} 
	
    name = 1000606name
    desc = 1000606desc
    style = 2
    picture = "ruins"
	
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 10
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

    action = {
		name = 1000606a
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }	
		command = { type = event which = 1000607 where = U40 when = 1 } #Trigger mass destruction event in RK states
		command = { type = event which = 1000607 where = U41 when = 1 } #Trigger mass destruction event in RK states
		command = { type = event which = 1000607 where = U42 when = 1 } #Trigger mass destruction event in RK states
		command = { type = event which = 1000607 where = U43 when = 1 } #Trigger mass destruction event in RK states
		command = { type = setflag which = RKRebels }  #Set flag for dynamic RK rebellions events (1000608 through 1000611)
    }
}

#### Events 1000608 through 1000611 used for dynamic rebellion events in RK states

#### Partisan uprising - U40 (RK Ostland) 
event = {
    id = 1000608
    random = no
    country = U40 
	persistent = yes
	
	#Trigger for first 19 times: flag = { which = [keyname] when = -1 value = 19 } #<= 19
	#Trigger for 20th time (and more than that): flag = { which = [keyname] when = 1 value = 20 } #>= 20
	#Command to increase +1 each time: type = setflag which = [keyname] when =1 value = 1 #increase by 1 the value of the flag each time
	
    name = 1000608name
    desc = 1000608desc
    style = 2
    picture = "partisans"
	
	trigger = { 
		flag = RKRebels
		random = 35
	} 
	
	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 60
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

    action = {
		trigger = {
            flag = { which = RKRebels when = -1 value = 20 }
        }
		name = 1000608a
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 when = 0 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 when = 0 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 when = 0 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 1000671 } #Refugees from the west event for SOV
		command = { type = setflag which = RKRebels when = 1 value = 1 }
	}
	
	action = {
        trigger = {
            flag = { which = RKRebels when = 1 value = 21 }
        }
        name = 1000608b	
        command = { type = dissent value = -10 }	
		command = { type = trigger which = 1000671 } #Refugees from the west event for SOV		
    }
}

#### Generalplan Ost - Eastern Colonization
event = {
	id = 1000612
	random = no
	country = GER
	persistent = yes

	decision = {
		event = 1000606 #Calm after the Storm event has happened
		flag = GeneralPlanOst
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		OR = {
				NOT = { flag = GPOstGotengau }
				NOT = { flag = GPOstMemel }
				NOT = { flag = GPOstIngermannland }
				NOT = { flag = GPOstBaku }
		}
	}
	
	decision_trigger = {
		manpower = 500
		ispuppet = U40
		ispuppet = U41
		ispuppet = U42
		ispuppet = U43
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = "Baltic States" country = -3 data = 1 } #All territories ceded from the Bitter Peace must be controlled, forces player to defeat all rebels
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Belarus country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = "Western Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Russia country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = "Southern Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Ukraine country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Kaukasus country = -3 data = 1 }
		area = { area = Arkhangelsk country = -3 data = 1 }
	}
	
	trigger = { 
		manpower = 500
		ispuppet = U40
		ispuppet = U41
		ispuppet = U42
		ispuppet = U43
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = "Baltic States" country = -3 data = 1 } #All territories ceded from the Bitter Peace must be controlled, forces player to defeat all rebels
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Belarus country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = "Western Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Russia country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = "Southern Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Ukraine country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Kaukasus country = -3 data = 1 }
		area = { area = Arkhangelsk country = -3 data = 1 } 
		} #Disable AI from taking this decision

	name = 1000612name
	desc = 1000612desc
	style = 2
	picture = "generalplanost"
	decision_picture = "generalplanostdecision"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { flag = GPOstGotengau } 
		} 
		name = 1000612a
		command = { type = trigger which = 1000613 }
	}
	
	action = {
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { flag = GPOstMemel } 
		} 
		name = 1000612b
		command = { type = trigger which = 1000614 }
	}
	
	action = {
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { flag = GPOstIngermannland } 
		} 
		name = 1000612c
		command = { type = trigger which = 1000615 }
	}
	
	action = {
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { flag = GPOstBaku } 
			control = { province = 713 data = U42 } # RK Kaukasus controls Baku, decision disabled if owned by Turkey
		} 
		name = 1000612d
		command = { type = trigger which = 1000616 }
	}
}

#### Generalplan Ost - Gotengau: Phase One
event = {
    id = 1000621
    random = no
    country = GER 
	save_date = yes
	
    name = 1000621name
    desc = 1000621desc
    style = 2
    picture = "gothiccastle"
	
	trigger = { 
		flag = GPOstGotengau
		ispuppet = U41
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 	
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Belarus country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Ukraine country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = "Southern Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		event = { id = 1000617 days = 455 } #Gotengau colonization decision enacted 1 year and 3 months ago (455 days)
	} 
	
	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

     action = {
		name = 1000621a
		#Gain cores in Crimean peninsula
		command = { type = addcore which = 637 where = U41 }
		command = { type = addcore which = 638 where = U41 }
		command = { type = addcore which = 639 where = U41 }
		command = { type = addcore which = 640 where = U41 }
		command = { type = addcore which = 641 where = U41 }
		#Restore penalties from colonization decision		
		command = { type = wartime_ic_mod value = 1 }
		command = { type = peacetime_ic_mod value = 0.5 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = free_manpower value = 0.02 }
	}
}

    id = 1000625
    random = no
    country = U41 
	
    name = 1000625name
    desc = 1000625desc
    style = 2
    picture = "rkukraine"
	
	trigger = { 
		flag = GPOstGotengau
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Belarus country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Ukraine country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = "Southern Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }		
		event = { id = 1000624 days = 180 } #Gotengau Phase Four event activated 6 months ago - 180 days (total combined time of 4 years 6 months) 
	} 
	
	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

     action = {
		name = 1000625a
		#Remove cores and claims from RK Ukraine, secede provinces to GER

		command = { type = removecore which = 613 where = U41 }

#### Generalplan Ost - Memel-Narew: Phase One
event = {
    id = 1000626
    random = no
    country = GER 
	save_date = yes
	
    name = 1000626name
    desc = 1000626desc
    style = 2
    picture = "bialystok"

	trigger = { 
		flag = GPOstMemel
		ispuppet = U40
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = "Baltic States" country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Belarus country = -3 data = 1 }
		event = { id = 1000618 days = 635 } #Memel-Narew colonization decision enacted 1 year 9 months ago (635 days)
	} 
	
	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

     action = {
		name = 1000626a
		#Gain cores in Bialystok area
		command = { type = addcore which = 250 }
		command = { type = addcore which = 252 }
		command = { type = addcore which = 253 }
		command = { type = addcore which = 254 }
		#Restore penalties from colonization decision		
		command = { type = wartime_ic_mod value = 1 }
		command = { type = peacetime_ic_mod value = 0.5 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = free_manpower value = 0.02 }
	}
}

#### Generalplan Ost - Baku: Phase One
event = {
    id = 1000637
    random = no
    country = GER 
	save_date = yes
	
    name = 1000637name
    desc = 1000637desc
    style = 2
    picture = "baku1"
	
	trigger = { 
		flag = GPOstBaku
		ispuppet = U42
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Kaukasus country = -3 data = 1 }
		event = { id = 1000620 days = 180 } #Baku colonization decision enacted 6 months ago (180 days)
	} 
	
	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

     action = {
		name = 1000637a
		#Development of facilities in Baku
		command = { type = oilpool value = 2000 }
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 713 value = 10 }
		command = { type = construct which = ic where = 713 value = 2 }
		command = { type = construct which = land_fort where = 713 value = 1 }
		command = { type = construct which = air_base where = 713 value = 2 }
		command = { type = construct which = radar_station where = 713 value = 1 }
		command = { type = construct which = flak where = 713 value = 2 }		
		#Restore penalties from colonization decision		
		command = { type = wartime_ic_mod value = 1 }
		command = { type = peacetime_ic_mod value = 0.5 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = free_manpower value = 0.02 }
	}
}

#### The Polish Question
event = {
	id = 1000641
	random = no
	country = GER
	save_date = yes

	decision = {
		event = 1000601 #Victory parade in Berlin 
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		ispuppet = U44
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 }
	}
	
	decision_trigger = {
		manpower = 500
		ispuppet = U44
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 232 size = 3 } #At least 3 units stationed in Warsaw
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 234 size = 3 } #At least 3 units stationed in Radom
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 235 size = 3 } #At least 3 units stationed in Krakow
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 238 size = 3 } #At least 3 units stationed in Stanislow
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 242 size = 3 } #At least 3 units stationed in Lwow
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 246 size = 3 } #At least 3 units stationed in Chelm
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = "Baltic States" country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Belarus country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Ukraine country = -3 data = 1 }
	}
	
	trigger = { 
		event = 1000601 #Victory parade in Berlin 
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		ispuppet = U44
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 } 
		}

	name = 1000641name
	desc = 1000641desc
	style = 2
	picture = "ggpoland"
	decision_picture = "ggpolanddecision"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 20
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		name = 1000641a
		command = { type = wartime_ic_mod value = -5 }
		command = { type = peacetime_ic_mod value = -2.5 }
		command = { type = manpowerpool value = -500 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = free_manpower value = -0.1 }
		command = { type = money value = -250 }
		command = { type = event which = 1000642 where = U44 when = 7 }
		command = { type = setflag which = GPOstPoland } #Flag set for integration of Poland
	}
	
	action = {
		name = 1000641b
		command = { type = relation which = U44 value = 10 }
	}
	
	action = {
		name = 1000641c
		command = { type = inherit which = U44 value = 1 }
	}
}

#### Operation Charlemagne
event = {
	id = 1000685
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = {
		exists = SOV
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = ENG } }
		ispuppet = U40
		ispuppet = U41
		ispuppet = U42
		ispuppet = U43
		event = { id = 1000600 days = 365 } #Treaty of Moscow happened 1 year ago	
	}
	
	decision_trigger = {
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = ENG } }
		NOT = { non_aggression = { country = GER country = SOV } } 
		event = { id = 1000600 days = 730 } #Treaty of Moscow happened 2 years ago	
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = "Baltic States" country = -3 data = 1 } #All territories ceded from the Bitter Peace must be controlled, forces player to defeat all rebels
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Belarus country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = "Western Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Russia country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = "Southern Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Ukraine country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Kaukasus country = -3 data = 1 }
		area = { area = Arkhangelsk country = -3 data = 1 }
		owned = { province = 548 data = -3 } #Vologda
	}
	
	trigger = { ai = no } #Disable AI from taking this decision

	name = 1000685name
	desc = 1000685desc
	style = 2
	picture = "charlemagne"
	decision_picture = "charlemagnedecision"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		name = 1000685a
		command = { type = war which = SOV }
		command = { type = setflag which = Charlemagne }
	}
}

#### Partition of the USSR (GER)
event = {
	id = 1000687
	random = no
	country = GER

	trigger = { 
		flag = Charlemagne
		NOT = { exists = SOV }
		NOT = { ispuppet = JAP } #JAP is NOT a puppet of GER to prevent event from firing if player annexes and releases JAP
		NOT = { event = 2011018 } #Event "Fading Sun" (defeat vs. China) has NOT fired
		NOT = { event = 2011028 } #Japan has not lost vs. USSR or USA
		NOT = { war = { country = JAP country = CHI } }
		NOT = { war = { country = JAP country = GER } }
	} 

	name = 1000687name
	desc = 1000687desc
	style = 2
	picture = "gerjappartition"

#### Partition of the USSR (JAP)

	id = 1000688
	random = no
	country = JAP

	name = 1000688name
	desc = 1000688desc
	style = 2
	picture = "gerjappartition"

	action = {
		name = 1000688a
		trigger = { alliance = { country = JAP country = GER } } #If JAP and GER are allied, secede provinces west of Yenisei River to GER
		command = { type = secederegion which = GER value = "Central Asia" when = 1 }
		command = { type = secederegion which = GER value = Kazakstan when = 1 }
		command = { type = secederegion which = GER value = Novosibirsk when = 1 }
		command = { type = secederegion which = GER value = Tomsk when = 1 }	
        command = { type = secederegion which = GER value = "Eastern Russia" when = 1 }
        command = { type = secederegion which = GER value = Urals when = 1 }
        command = { type = secederegion which = GER value = "Northern Russia" when = 1 }	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 1156 when = 1 } # Krasnoyarsk
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 1152 when = 1 } # Salekhard	
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U41 value = 660 when = 1 } # Ensure RK Ukraine receives its claims
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U41 value = 666 when = 1 }	# Ensure RK Ukraine receives its claims	
		#Add claims for JAP and MAN on Siberia to ensure that Siberian puppet doesn't auto-trade for its claimed/core provinces
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1191 where = MAN }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1196 where = MAN }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1193 where = MAN }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1192 where = MAN }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1194 where = MAN }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1195 where = MAN }		
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1190 where = MAN }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1185 where = MAN }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1187 where = MAN }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1188 where = MAN }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1175 where = MAN }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1171 where = MAN }

	id = 1000701
	random = no
	tag = { GER JAP }
	persistent = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			war = { country = GER country = SOV }
			event = 2007033 #Bitter Peace
		}
		event = 2011005 #Japan has signed the Tripartite Pact (germany.txt)
		event = 2006002 #Italy has signed the Tripartite Pact (germany.txt)
		NOT = { event = 2011018 } #"The Fading Sun" event has NOT fired (japan.txt)
		NOT = { local_flag = GERJAPAgreement }
		random = 25
	}

	name = 1000701name
	desc = 1000701desc
	style = 2
	picture = "asianpartition"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1941 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		name = 1000701a

		command = { trigger = { country = GER } type = relation which = JAP value = 20 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = GERJAPAgreement }
	}
}

#### The Swedish Question
event = {

	decision = { 
		exists = SWE

		event = 1000601 #Event "Victory Parade in Berlin" has fired

#### The Swiss Question
event = {
	id = 1000722
	random = no
	country = GER
	
	decision = { 
		exists = SCH 
		NOT = { alliance = { country = GER country = SCH } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = ENG } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SCH } }
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } #Total domination of Europe and successful Barbarossa required
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = France country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = England country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Scotland country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Belarus country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Ukraine country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = "Southern Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		#region = { region = Denmark country = -3 data = 1 } #Removed Scandinavian requirement in case player specifically not choose war with these countries
		#region = { region = Norway country = -3 data = 1 }
		#region = { region = Sweden country = -3 data = 1 }
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SCH } }
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 98 size = 3 } #Surround Switzerland
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 97 size = 3 }
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 105 size = 3 }
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 132 size = 3 }
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 189 size = 3 }
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 402 size = 3 }
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 395 size = 3 }	
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 407 size = 3 }
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 398 size = 3 }
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 91 size = 3 }	
	}
	
	trigger = { 
		exists = SCH 
		NOT = { alliance = { country = GER country = SCH } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = ENG } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SCH } }
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } #Total domination of Europe and successful Barbarossa required
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = France country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = England country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Scotland country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Belarus country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Ukraine country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = "Southern Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		}

	name = 1000722name
	desc = 1000722desc
	style = 2
	picture = "swissbook"
	decision_picture = "swissdecision"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		name = 1000722a
		command = { type = belligerence which = GER value = 20 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = war which = SCH }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = ai_prepare_war which = SCH }
		command = { type = trigger which = 1000723 }
	}
	
	action = {
		name = 1000722b
		command = { type = relation which = SCH value = 50 }
	}

#### Partition of Switzerland
event = {
    id = 1000725
    random = no
    country = GER 
	
    name = 1000725name
    desc = 1000725desc
    style = 2
    picture = "swisspartition"

	trigger = {  
		NOT = { war = { country = SCH country = GER } }
		region = { region = Switzerland country = -3 data = 1 }
		OR = { 
			exists = U52
			exists = U55
		}
	} 
	
	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 7
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

    action = {
		name = 1000725a
		command = { type = dissent value = -1 }
		command = { trigger = { alliance = { country = GER country = ITA } } type = secedeprovince which = ITA value = 390 when = 2 } #Lugano
		command = { trigger = { alliance = { country = GER country = ITA } } type = relation which = ITA value = 30 } #Lugano
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { alliance = { country = GER country = ITA } } } type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 390 when = 2 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { alliance = { country = GER country = ITA } } } type = addclaim which = 390 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 392 when = 2 } #Zurich
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 389 when = 2 } #Bern
		command = { trigger = { control = { province = 98 data = U52 } } type = secedeprovince which = U52 value = 391 when = 2 } #Geneva to Burgundy if they already control Pontarlier
		command = { trigger = { control = { province = 98 data = U55 } } type = secedeprovince which = U55 value = 391 when = 2 } #Geneva to French State if they already control Pontarlier
		command = { trigger = { control = { province = 98 data = U55 } } type = addclaim which = U55 value = 391 }
		#Deconstruct forts in Switzerland
		command = { type = construct which = land_fort where = 390 value = -10 }
		command = { type = construct which = land_fort where = 389 value = -10 }
		command = { type = construct which = land_fort where = 391 value = -10 }
		command = { type = construct which = land_fort where = 392 value = -10 }
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 390 value = 30 }
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 389 value = 30 }
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 391 value = 30 }
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 392 value = 10 }
		command = { type = supplies value = 2500 }
		command = { type = metalpool value = 5000 }
	}
	
	action = {
		name = 1000725b
		command = { trigger = { alliance = { country = GER country = ITA } } type = relation which = ITA value = -30 }
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 390 when = 2 } #Lugano
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 392 when = 2 } #Zurich
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 389 when = 2 } #Bern
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = GER value = 391 when = 2 } #Geneva
		command = { type = addclaim which = 390 }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 391 }
		#Deconstruct forts in Switzerland
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 390 value = 30 }
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 389 value = 30 }
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 391 value = 30 }
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 392 value = 10 }

event = {
	id = 1000727
	random = no
	country = GER
	
	decision = { 
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = ENG } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = USA } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = JAP } }
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } #Total domination of Europe and successful Barbarossa required
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = France country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = England country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Scotland country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Denmark country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Norway country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Sweden country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = "Baltic States" country = -3 data = 1 } #All territories ceded from the Bitter Peace must be controlled
		region = { region = Poland country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Belarus country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = "Western Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Russia country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = "Southern Russia" country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Ukraine country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Kaukasus country = -3 data = 1 }
		area = { area = Arkhangelsk country = -3 data = 1 }
		NOT = { exists = SOV } #Soviet Union has been destroyed
		NOT = { event = 2049051 } #USA surrenders to Germany vanilla event
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = USA } }
		NOT = { non_aggression = { country = GER country = USA } }
	}
	
	trigger = { ai = no } #Disable AI from taking this decision

	name = 1000727name
	desc = 1000727desc
	style = 2
	picture = "usainvasion"
	decision_picture = "invadeamericadecision"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		name = 1000727a
		command = { type = belligerence which = GER value = 10 }
		command = { type = war which = USA }
	}
	
	action = {
		name = 1000727b
		command = { type = relation which = USA value = 25 }
		command = { type = non_aggression which = USA where = GER }
	}
}

#### The Irish Question
event = {
	id = 1000911
	random = no
	country = GER
	
	decision = {
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 } 
		control = { province = 35 data = -3 } #Northern Ireland
		control = { province = 36 data = -3 } #Northern Ireland
		NOT = { exists = U71 }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = IRE } }
	}
	
	decision_trigger = {
		region = { region = England country = -3 data = 1 } #Control all of England
		region = { region = Scotland country = -3 data = 1 } #Control all of Scotland
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 35 size = 1 } #At least 1 unit stationed in Londonderry
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 36 size = 1 } #At least 1 unit stationed in Belfast
	}
	
	trigger = { 
		control = { province = 35 data = -3 }
		control = { province = 36 data = -3 }
	} 
	
	name = "1000911name"
	desc = "1000911desc"
	style = 2
	picture = "irishnazis"
	decision_picture = "ireland_axis"
	
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1939 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }
	
	action = {
		name = 1000911a
		ai_chance = 90
		trigger = { exists = IRE }
		command = { type = relation which = IRE value = 150 }
		command = { type = alliance which = IRE when = 0 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = IRE value = 35 when = 2 } # Londonderry
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = IRE value = 36 when = 2 } # Belfast
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { exists = IRE } } type = independence which = IRE value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { exists = IRE } } type = make_puppet which = IRE value = 1 }
	}
	
	action = {
		name = 1000911b
		ai_chance = 5
		trigger = { exists = IRE }
		command = { type = relation which = IRE value = 200 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = IRE value = 35 when = 2 } # Londonderry
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = IRE value = 36 when = 2 } # Belfast
	}
	
	action = {
		name = 1000911c
		ai_chance = 5
		trigger = { exists = IRE }
		command = { type = relation which = IRE value = -75 }
		command = { type = independence which = U71 value = 1 }
		command = { type = make_puppet which = U71 }
	}
	
	action = {
		name = 1000911d
		trigger = { NOT = { exists = IRE } } #Option is only available if IRE no longer exists (annexed by player)
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = independence which = IRE value = 1 }
		command = { type = make_puppet which = IRE }
	}
	
	action = {
		name = 1000911e
		ai_chance = 0
		trigger = { exists = IRE }
		command = { type = relation which = IRE value = -100 }
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
	}
}

	country = IRE

		event = 1000911 #The Irish Question

	} 
	
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1939 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

		command = { type = set_domestic which = free_market value = 4 }

#### The Germans are preparing an airborne assault! (Airborne Infantry 1941)
event = {
	id = 1000917
	random = no
	country = ENG
	
	trigger = { 
		ai = yes
		OR = {
			technology = { country = GER value = 1680 } # Airborne Infantry 1941
			AND = {
				region = { region = Ireland country = -2 data = 1 value = 10 } #Hostile countries control 10% or more of Ireland
				paratrooper = { country = GER value = 1 when = now } #Germany has at least 1 paratrooper division
				transport_plane = { country = GER value = 1 when = now } #Germany has at least 1 transport plane division
			}
		}
		flag = sealionevents
		NOT = { ai = GER }
		war = { country = GER country = ENG }
	} 

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1939 }
	offset = 3 #Offset must be low to prevent player from quickly using paratrooper to occupy empty British provinces
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }
	
	name = 1000917name
	desc = 1000917desc
	style = 2
	picture = "dunkirk"

	action = {
		name = 1000917a
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = manpowerpool value = -150 }
		#Activate Garrison with AA brigades on all non-beach provinces in the UK, prevents player from landing paratroopers with no resistance
		command = { type = activate_division which = 12700 value = 10068 where = 4 when = 0 } #Activate 1. Home Guard Anti-Air
		command = { type = activate_division which = 12700 value = 10069 where = 5 when = 0 } #Activate 2. Home Guard Anti-Air
		command = { type = activate_division which = 12700 value = 10070 where = 6 when = 0 } #Activate 3. Home Guard Anti-Air
		command = { type = activate_division which = 12700 value = 10071 where = 7 when = 0 } #Activate 4. Home Guard Anti-Air
		command = { type = activate_division which = 12700 value = 10072 where = 8 when = 0 } #Activate 5. Home Guard Anti-Air
		command = { type = activate_division which = 12700 value = 10073 where = 10 when = 0 } #Activate 6. Home Guard Anti-Air
		command = { type = activate_division which = 12700 value = 10074 where = 13 when = 0 } #Activate 7. Home Guard Anti-Air
		command = { type = activate_division which = 12700 value = 10075 where = 14 when = 0 } #Activate 8. Home Guard Anti-Air
		command = { type = activate_division which = 12700 value = 10076 where = 15 when = 0 } #Activate 9. Home Guard Anti-Air

#### Concentrate the Royal Navy on home defense 
event = {
	id = 1000920
	random = no
	country = ENG
	
	trigger = { 
		ai = yes
		war = { country = GER country = ENG }
		OR = { 
			AND = {
				event = 1000914 #ENG has noticed Germany has Marines 1940 technology
				event = 1000915 #ENG has noticed Germany has Troopship 1941 technology
				event = 1000916 #ENG has noticed Germany has Amphibious Assault 1942 technology
			}
			AND = {
				event = 2007033 #Bitter peace 
				event = 1000672 #Event "The USSR has surrendered" has fired
			}
			AND = {
				transport = { country = GER value = 15 when = now } #Fire if GER has over X number of Transport ships in case player goes for Sealion before Barbarossa
				marine = { country = GER value = 5 when = now } 	#Fire if GER has over X number of Marine divisions in case player goes for Sealion before Barbarossa
			}
		} 
	}
	
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 10
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }
	
	name = 1000920name
	desc = 1000920desc
	style = 2
	picture = "royal_navy"

	action = {
		name = 1000920a
		command = { type = ai which = "switch/ENG_Home_Defense.ai" } #AI switch to instruct the British AI to focus all of its naval units on home defense
	}
}

	country = GER
	save_date = yes

		ai = ENG
		war = { country = GER country = ENG }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		event = { id = 1000600 days = 75 } #Treaty of Moscow happened 75 days ago
		NOT = { event = 1000919 } #Germany has NOT landed on the British Isles
		NOT = { event = 1000927 } #Germany has NOT landed on the isles and given the UK one last chance to come to terms
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 }		
	}
